### [55] [Reward Sharpness-Aware Fine-Tuning for Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21175)
*Kwanyoung Kim,Byeongsu Sim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对奖励中心扩散强化学习（RDRL）容易受到奖励黑客攻击的问题，提出了一种新的方法RSA-FT，通过利用稳健化奖励模型的梯度来缓解此问题，并且不需要重新训练该模型。实验表明，这种方法能够独立地减轻奖励黑客行为并提高鲁棒性，而联合使用时效果更佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管扩散模型可以生成高质量输出，但基于奖励的扩散强化学习（RDRL）仍然容易遭受奖励黑客攻击，即在感知质量没有相应改善的情况下奖励分数增加。这种脆弱性源于奖励模型梯度不够稳健，特别是在输入图像对应的奖励景观非常陡峭时。为了解决这个问题，研究者们探索了如何利用一个更加稳健化的奖励模型梯度而不必重训这个模型的方法。

Method: 研究者们引入了几种方法来利用经过调整后的奖励模型梯度，其中包括通过对扩散模型参数进行扰动以及对其生成样本施加扰动来获得平滑处理后的奖励模型梯度。这些方法单独使用时就能缓解奖励黑客问题并增强系统鲁棒性；当它们一起使用时，则能进一步放大这些好处。

Result: 实验证明，所提出的方法单独或结合使用都能有效减少奖励黑客现象，并提高了系统的鲁棒性和可靠性。

Conclusion: 提出的框架RSA-FT（Reward Sharpness-Aware Fine-Tuning）简单、广泛兼容，并且能够持续提升RDRL的可靠性。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) has proven effective in aligning large language models with human preferences, inspiring the development of reward-centric diffusion reinforcement learning (RDRL) to achieve similar alignment and controllability. While diffusion models can generate high-quality outputs, RDRL remains susceptible to reward hacking, where the reward score increases without corresponding improvements in perceptual quality. We demonstrate that this vulnerability arises from the non-robustness of reward model gradients, particularly when the reward landscape with respect to the input image is sharp. To mitigate this issue, we introduce methods that exploit gradients from a robustified reward model without requiring its retraining. Specifically, we employ gradients from a flattened reward model, obtained through parameter perturbations of the diffusion model and perturbations of its generated samples. Empirically, each method independently alleviates reward hacking and improves robustness, while their joint use amplifies these benefits. Our resulting framework, RSA-FT (Reward Sharpness-Aware Fine-Tuning), is simple, broadly compatible, and consistently enhances the reliability of RDRL.

### [56] [Prompt replay: speeding up grpo with on-policy reuse of high-signal prompts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21177)
*Andrei Baroian,Rutger Berger*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Prompt Replay的方法，用于GRPO中的在线数据选择，旨在通过重用具有中等难度的提示来提高学习信号和优化策略。实验结果表明，该方法在减少零方差提示、增加绝对优势以及加快初始准确性提升方面表现出色。然而，在使用过于激进的配置时，其性能会趋于平稳并最终与基线收敛。此外，研究还发现Qwen2.5-Math模型存在虚假奖励效应，这可能影响其作为GRPO方法研究唯一测试平台的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的GRPO风格训练由于昂贵的rollouts而浪费了大量的计算资源，并且产生了许多无法使用的提示。为了解决这个问题，作者提出了一个无额外开销的在线数据选择方法——Prompt Replay，它仅重用提示而不重用整个轨迹，以此保持在线策略优化的同时提高效率。

Method: Prompt Replay方法通过在每一步后将中等难度的提示插入缓冲区，并优先考虑接近0.5通过率（即一半答案正确，一半错误）的提示，从而最大化优势。训练批次由重用的提示和新样本混合而成，通过冷却步骤和最大重用次数来控制激进程度与过拟合风险之间的平衡。

Result: 实验证明，Prompt Replay能够减少零方差提示的数量、增加平均绝对优势并且显示出更快的初始准确度增长速度。但是，当配置过于激进时，它的表现会达到一个平台期并最终与基线一致。对于某些模型家族（如Llama-3.2-3B, Qwen3-8B）及训练数据集（Dolci, Polaris），这种方法特别有效。

Conclusion: Prompt Replay是一种有效的在线数据选择技术，适用于那些rollouts为主要瓶颈且数据集对模型来说较为困难的情况。尽管如此，为了防止过早收敛到局部最优解，需要谨慎调整相关参数。同时，研究者也应警惕特定模型（如Qwen2.5-Math）中可能出现的虚假奖励现象。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) plays a crucial role in expanding the capacities of LLM reasoning, but GRPO-style training is dominated by expensive rollouts and wastes compute on unusable prompts. We propose Prompt Replay, an overhead-free online data selection method for GRPO that reuses prompts only (not trajectories), to preserve on-policy optimization. After each step, we insert prompts with medium difficulty into a buffer, and prioritize prompts closer to a pass rate of 0.5 (half answers correct, half wrong) to maximize the advantage, thus learning signal. Training batches are formed by mixing reused prompts with fresh samples, with cooldown steps and max reuse times controlling aggressiveness vs risk of overfitting. Across multiple model families (Llama-3.2- 3B, Qwen3-8B) and training datasets (Dolci, Polaris), evaluated using average accuracy on six standard math benchmarks, Prompt Replay reduces zero-variance prompts, increases mean absolute advantage and shows faster initial accuracy gains. Yet, it plateaus and converges with the baseline, as too aggressive configuration was used. The method is most efficient when the rollouts are the primary bottleneck and the dataset is difficult for the model. We additionally observe that Qwen2.5-Math can exhibit spurious-reward effects that invalidates ablations, raising a warning signal for using it as a sole testbed for GRPO method research.

### [57] [On the Role of Batch Size in Stochastic Conditional Gradient Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21191)
*Rustem Islamov,Roman Machacek,Aurelien Lucchi,Antonio Silveti-Falls,Eduard Gorbunov,Volkan Cevher*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在$μ$-Kurdyka-Łojasiewicz条件下，随机条件梯度方法中批量大小的作用。通过分析基于动量的算法（如Scion），揭示了批量大小、步长和随机噪声之间的相互作用，并发现批量大小对优化准确性的影响呈现阶段依赖性：初始增加有助于提高精度，但超过一定阈值后效果饱和甚至可能降低性能。基于这些理论，提出了选择批量大小和步长的原则性指导以及一种自适应策略，在保持收敛保证的同时于训练过程中动态调整批量大小和序列长度。实验结果与理论预测一致，为大规模优化中的高效训练计划设计提供了理论框架和指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索批量大小对于基于动量的随机条件梯度方法（例如Scion）在$μ$-KL条件下优化性能的影响机制，并据此提供有效的批量大小和步长选取原则及自适应调整策略以提升大规模优化任务的效率。

Method: 通过对基于动量的随机条件梯度算法进行新分析，明确捕捉到步长、批量大小与随机噪声间的交互作用；提出了一种能够随训练过程逐步增大批量大小及序列长度同时确保收敛性的自适应策略。

Result: 研究表明，存在一个关于批量大小影响优化准确性的阶段依赖行为：开始时增加批量大小可以改善性能，但超过某个临界点后继续增大反而可能导致性能下降。此外，还确定了最优步长大小，并观察到该理论与大规模训练实践中的经验做法相符。

Conclusion: 本文为理解随机条件梯度方法中批量大小缩放效应提供了理论框架，并为大规模优化任务下制定高效的训练计划提供了具体指导。

Abstract: We study the role of batch size in stochastic conditional gradient methods under a $μ$-Kurdyka-Łojasiewicz ($μ$-KL) condition. Focusing on momentum-based stochastic conditional gradient algorithms (e.g., Scion), we derive a new analysis that explicitly captures the interaction between stepsize, batch size, and stochastic noise. Our study reveals a regime-dependent behavior: increasing the batch size initially improves optimization accuracy but, beyond a critical threshold, the benefits saturate and can eventually degrade performance under a fixed token budget. Notably, the theory predicts the magnitude of the optimal stepsize and aligns well with empirical practices observed in large-scale training. Leveraging these insights, we derive principled guidelines for selecting the batch size and stepsize, and propose an adaptive strategy that increases batch size and sequence length during training while preserving convergence guarantees. Experiments on NanoGPT are consistent with the theoretical predictions and illustrate the emergence of the predicted scaling regimes. Overall, our results provide a theoretical framework for understanding batch size scaling in stochastic conditional gradient methods and offer guidance for designing efficient training schedules in large-scale optimization.

</details>


### [58] [Sonny: Breaking the Compute Wall in Medium-Range Weather Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21284)
*Minjong Cheon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 介绍了一种名为Sonny的高效层次化transformer，用于中长期天气预报，在计算资源有限的情况下仍能达到与现有业务系统相当的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管基于深度学习的数据驱动天气预报方法表现出色，但它们通常需要大量的训练数据和计算密集型架构，这为计算资源有限的研究团队带来了实际障碍。

Method: 提出了一种名为Sonny的两阶段StepsNet设计模型，其中狭窄慢路径首先建模大规模大气动力学，随后全宽快速路径整合热力学交互作用。此外，通过在训练过程中应用指数移动平均（EMA）来稳定中期滚动预测，而无需额外的微调步骤。

Result: Sonny在WeatherBench2上的表现证明了其强大的中程预报能力，与业务基准相比保持竞争力，并且在延长的热带预报时间上相对于FastNet显示出了明显的优势。实际上，使用单个NVIDIA A40 GPU大约5.5天即可完成对Sonny的训练直至收敛。

Conclusion: Sonny提供了一种有效的解决方案，能够在不大幅增加计算成本的前提下实现高质量的中程天气预报。

Abstract: Weather forecasting is a fundamental problem for protecting lives and infrastructure from high-impact atmospheric events. Recently, data-driven weather forecasting methods based on deep learning have demonstrated strong performance, often reaching accuracy levels competitive with operational numerical systems. However, many existing models rely on large-scale training regimes and compute-intensive architectures, which raises the practical barrier for academic groups with limited compute resources. Here we introduce Sonny, an efficient hierarchical transformer that achieves competitive medium-range forecasting performance while remaining feasible within reasonable compute budgets. At the core of Sonny is a two-stage StepsNet design: a narrow slow path first models large-scale atmospheric dynamics, and a subsequent full-width fast path integrates thermodynamic interactions. To stabilize medium-range rollout without an additional fine-tuning stage, we apply exponential moving average (EMA) during training. On WeatherBench2, Sonny yields robust medium-range forecast skill, remains competitive with operational baselines, and demonstrates clear advantages over FastNet, particularly at extended tropical lead times. In practice, Sonny can be trained to convergence on a single NVIDIA A40 GPU in approximately 5.5 days.

</details>

### [60] [WN-Wrangle: Wireless Network Data Wrangling Assistant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21310)
*Anirudh Kamath,Dustin Maas,Jacobus Van der Merwe,Anna Fariha*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: This paper introduces WN-Wrangle, an interactive assistant for wrangling wireless network datasets. It addresses the unique challenges of integrating temporally ordered, multi-source data and enforces domain-specific semantics to improve data quality.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to address the time-consuming and complex task of data wrangling in the context of wireless network data, which involves integrating multiple, temporally ordered tables with specific domain knowledge that existing tools do not adequately support.

Method: WN-Wrangle, an interactive data wrangling assistant, is designed specifically for the wireless network domain. It suggests the top-k next-best wrangling operations by enforcing temporal constraints and incorporating a mechanism aware of wireless network semantics to score and rank wrangling operators.

Result: WN-Wrangle is shown to effectively identify and resolve data-quality issues specific to wireless network datasets, providing accurate suggestions for wrangling steps over real-world datasets from the POWDER city-scale wireless testbed.

Conclusion: WN-Wrangle offers a tailored solution for the efficient and effective wrangling of wireless network datasets, overcoming the limitations of generic data wrangling techniques by leveraging domain-specific knowledge and temporal ordering.

Abstract: Data wrangling continues to be the most time-consuming task in the data science pipeline and wireless network data is no exception. Prior approaches for automatic or assisted data-wrangling primarily target unordered, single-table data. However, unlike traditional datasets where rows in a table are unordered and assumed to be independent of each other, wireless network datasets are often collected across multiple measurement devices, producing multiple, temporally ordered tables that must be integrated for obtaining the complete dataset. For instance, to create a dataset of the signal quality of 5G cell towers within a geographic region, GPS data collected by cellphones must be joined with radio frequency measurements of the corresponding cell towers. However, the join key timestamp typically exhibits mismatched sampling periods, causing a misalignment. Data wrangling techniques for generic time-series datasets also fail here, since they lack knowledge of domain-specific data semantics, which are often defined by network protocols and system configurations. To aid in wrangling wireless network datasets, we demonstrate WN-Wrangle, an interactive wrangling assistant, tailored to the wireless network domain that suggests the top-k next-best wrangling operations, along with rich, domain-specific explanations. Under the hood, WN-Wrangle enforces temporal constraints- and a wireless network semantics-aware mechanism to score and rank an extended set of wrangling operators to improve the data quality. We demonstrate how WN-Wrangle identifies elusive data-quality issues specific to the wireless network domain and suggests accurate wrangling steps over datasets obtained from the widely used POWDER city-scale wireless testbed.

</details>


### [61] [FGIM: a Fast Graph-based Indexes Merging Framework for Approximate Nearest Neighbor Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21710)
*Zekai Wu,Jiabao Jin,Peng Cheng,Xiaoyao Zhong,Lei Chen,Yongxin Tong,Zhitao Shen,Jingkuan Song,Heng Tao Shen,Xuemin Lin*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种快速图索引合并框架FGIM，该框架通过三种核心技术：邻近图到k最近邻图的转换、k最近邻图的优化以及k最近邻图到邻近图的转换来合并多个现有的基于图的索引。实验结果表明，与最新的ANNS方法相比，FGIM框架在保持搜索性能的同时，实现了显著的速度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有大量工作专注于设计高效的基于图的近似最近邻搜索(ANNS)方法，但本文着眼于现实世界中一个重要且较少被关注的问题：如何将多个现有的基于图的索引合并成一个统一的索引。这在分布式系统中的集群整合和实时向量数据库中的读写竞争等场景下尤为重要。

Method: 提出了Fast Graph-based Indexes Merging (FGIM)框架，包含三个核心步骤：1. 通过跨查询从输入的基于图的索引中提取潜在候选邻居的Proximity Graphs (PGs) 到 k Nearest Neighbor Graph ($k$-NNG) 转换；2. $k$-NNG 精炼，用于识别被忽视的高质量邻居并保持图连通性；3. $k$-NNG 到 PG 转换，旨在提高图可导航性和增强搜索性能。

Result: 在六个真实数据集上的广泛实验显示，FGIM框架适用于各种主流基于图的ANNS方法，并且对于没有增量支持的方法平均达到7.9倍的速度提升，同时对HNSW的增量构建实现高达3.5倍的速度提升，同时保持了可比或更优的搜索性能。

Conclusion: 通过引入FGIM框架，研究展示了有效合并多个基于图的索引的可能性，这对于需要高效处理高维数据检索的应用来说是一项重要的进步。该解决方案不仅提高了现有方法的速度，而且保证了良好的搜索质量。

Abstract: As the state-of-the-art methods for high-dimensional data retrieval, Approximate Nearest Neighbor Search (ANNS) approaches with graph-based indexes have attracted increasing attention and play a crucial role in many real-world applications, e.g., retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) and recommendation systems. Unlike the extensive works focused on designing efficient graph-based ANNS methods, this paper delves into merging multiple existing graph-based indexes into a single one, which is also crucial in many real-world scenarios (e.g., cluster consolidation in distributed systems and read-write contention in real-time vector databases). We propose a Fast Graph-based Indexes Merging (FGIM) framework with three core techniques: (1) Proximity Graphs (PGs) to $k$ Nearest Neighbor Graph ($k$-NNG) transformation used to extract potential candidate neighbors from input graph-based indexes through cross-querying, (2) $k$-NNG refinement designed to identify overlooked high-quality neighbors and maintain graph connectivity, and (3) $k$-NNG to PG transformation aimed at improving graph navigability and enhancing search performance. Then, we integrate our FGIM framework with the state-of-the-art ANNS method, HNSW, and other existing mainstream graph-based methods to demonstrate its generality and merging efficiency. Extensive experiments on six real-world datasets show that our FGIM framework is applicable to various mainstream graph-based ANNS methods, achieves up to 3.5$\times$ speedup over HNSW's incremental construction and an average of 7.9$\times$ speedup for methods without incremental support, while maintaining comparable or superior search performance.

</details>


### [62] [Approximate Butterfly Counting in Sublinear Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21816)
*Chi Luo,Jiaxin Song,Yuhao Zhang,Kai Wang,Zhixing He,Kuan Yang*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种两层采样算法TLS，用于在查询模型下估计二分图中的蝴蝶数量。该算法通过限制访问的图结构来显著降低查询成本，并引入了新的技术以确保理论保证。实验结果表明，与现有解决方案相比，TLS在查询成本和运行时间上可降低三个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在分析二分图时，蝴蝶计数是一个基本的研究问题，但现有的算法通常需要访问整个图的大部分，这在处理非常大的图时面临挑战，因为I/O成本很高。因此，研究者们旨在开发一种能够在有限访问图结构的情况下准确估计蝴蝶数量的新方法。

Method: 提出了名为TLS的两层采样算法，它允许执行度查询、邻居查询及顶点对查询等操作。此外，还结合了几种关键的技术来控制方差，比如“先小度采样”、“通过小子集进行楔形采样”。为了提供理论上的保证，进一步引入了“重-轻分割”和“猜测-证明”两种新技术。

Result: 证明了对于任意给定的近似参数0 < eps < 1，该算法可以在一般二分图上达到(1+eps)的精度，并且具有承诺的时间和查询复杂度。特别是当输入图足够密集时，承诺的时间是次线性的。通过对15个数据集进行广泛实验，展示了TLS相较于现有方案，在提供稳健估计的同时，其查询成本和运行时间降低了多达三个数量级。

Conclusion: TLS算法为解决大规模二分图中蝴蝶计数问题提供了一个高效且实用的方法，特别适用于I/O成本高昂的情形。通过创新性地结合多种技术手段，TLS不仅提高了准确性也极大地减少了所需资源。

Abstract: Bipartite graphs serve as a natural model for representing relationships between two different types of entities. When analyzing bipartite graphs, butterfly counting is a fundamental research problem that aims to count the number of butterflies (i.e., 2x2 bicliques) in a given bipartite graph. While this problem has been extensively studied in the literature, existing algorithms usually necessitate access to a large portion of the entire graph, presenting challenges in real scenarios where graphs are extremely large and I/O costs are expensive. In this paper, we study the butterfly counting problem under the query model, where the following query operations are permitted: degree query, neighbor query, and vertex-pair query. We propose TLS, a practical two-level sampling algorithm that can estimate the butterfly count accurately while accessing only a limited graph structure, achieving significantly lower query costs under the standard query model. TLS also incorporates several key techniques to control the variance, including "small-degree-first sampling" and "wedge sampling via small subsets". To ensure theoretical guarantees, we further introduce two novel techniques: "heavy-light partition" and "guess-and-prove", integrated into TLS. With these techniques, we prove that the algorithm can achieve a (1+eps) accuracy for any given approximation parameter 0 < eps < 1 on general bipartite graphs with a promised time and query complexity. In particular, the promised time is sublinear when the input graph is dense enough. Extensive experiments on 15 datasets demonstrate that TLS delivers robust estimates with up to three orders of magnitude lower query costs and runtime compared to existing solutions.

### [63] [Accelerating Fresh Data Exploration with Fluid ETL Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22220)
*Maxwell Norfolk,Dong Xie*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的数据摄入系统，称为流式ETL管道，它允许用户根据需要启动或停止任意的数据预处理例程而不会阻塞数据摄入，从而利用偶尔的空闲系统容量或廉价的抢占式资源来加速未来的探索查询，并适应用户不断变化的兴趣。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 面对新鲜数据探索的需求增长以及传统ETL管道在处理快速积累的数据时存在的资源密集型问题，研究者们希望通过一种新方法来解决这些问题，即通过利用系统的空闲容量或低成本资源来改善数据处理效率和灵活性。

Method: 引入了一种名为流式ETL管道的新类型数据摄入系统，该系统支持按需启动/停止任何数据预处理例程（DPRs），并且不会中断数据摄入过程。

Result: 实验结果证明了流式ETL管道的概念是可行的，同时也指出了这一新方法所带来的关于临时查询处理、DPR生成与管理等任务的新挑战。

Conclusion: 流式ETL管道为提高数据探索过程中对不可预测的数据特征及分析目标的适应性提供了一个有前景的方向，但其实施还面临着一些开放的研究挑战。

Abstract: Recently, we have seen an increasing need for fresh data exploration, where data analysts seek to explore the main characteristics or detect anomalies of data being actively collected. In addition to the common challenges in classic data exploration, such as a lack of prior knowledge about the data or the analysis goal, fresh data exploration also demands an ingestion system with sufficient throughput to keep up with rapid data accumulation. However, leveraging traditional Extract-Transform-Load (ETL) pipelines to achieve low query latency can still be extremely resource-intensive as they must conduct an excessive amount of data preprocessing routines (DPRs) (e.g., parsing and indexing) to cover unpredictable data characteristics and analysis goals. To overcome this challenge, we seek to approach it from a different angle: leveraging occasional idle system capacity or cheap preemptive resources (e.g., Amazon Spot Instance) during ingestion. In particular, we introduce a new type of data ingestion system called fluid ETL pipelines, which allow users to start/stop arbitrary DPRs on demand without blocking data ingestion. With fluid ETL pipelines, users can start potentially useful DPRs to accelerate future exploration queries whenever idle/cheap resources are available. Moreover, users can dynamically change which DPRs to run with limited resources to adapt to users' evolving interests. We conducted experiments on a real-world dataset and verified that our vision is viable. The introduction of fluid ETL pipelines also raises new challenges in handling essential tasks, such as ad-hoc query processing, DPR generation, and DPR management. In this paper, we discuss open research challenges in detail and outline potential directions for addressing them.

</details>

### [64] [HCAG: Hierarchical Abstraction and Retrieval-Augmented Generation on Theoretical Repositories with LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20299)
*Yusen Wu,Xiaotie Deng*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为HCAG的框架，用于改进复杂代码库（如算法博弈论中的代码库）的检索增强生成方法。该框架通过两阶段设计和多层次知识结构来提高代码质量和架构一致性，并通过实验验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的检索增强生成(RAG)方法在处理复杂的、理论驱动的代码库时，难以捕捉高层次的架构模式和跨文件依赖性，导致抽象概念与可执行实现之间存在持续的语义和结构差距。

Method: 提出了Hierarchical Code/Architecture-guided Agent Generation (HCAG)框架，采用两阶段设计：离线层次抽象阶段递归解析代码仓库及对齐的理论文本以构建多分辨率语义知识库；在线层次检索和脚手架生成阶段则进行自顶向下的逐层检索以指导LLMs按照先架构后模块的方式生成代码。此外还引入了一个受合作博弈启发的多智能体讨论机制以进一步提高鲁棒性和一致性。

Result: 广泛的实验表明，在多样化的博弈论系统生成任务中，HCAG在代码质量、架构一致性和需求通过率方面显著优于代表性的仓库级方法。同时，HCAG还能产生大规模对齐的理论-实现数据集，有效提升领域特定大模型的语言模型性能。

Conclusion: 尽管HCAG是在算法博弈论背景下展示的，但其也为其他领域内从结构化代码库中挖掘、重用和生成复杂系统提供了一般蓝图。

Abstract: Existing Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) methods for code struggle to capture the high-level architectural patterns and cross-file dependencies inherent in complex, theory-driven codebases, such as those in algorithmic game theory (AGT), leading to a persistent semantic and structural gap between abstract concepts and executable implementations. To address this challenge, we propose Hierarchical Code/Architecture-guided Agent Generation (HCAG), a framework that reformulates repository-level code generation as a structured, planning-oriented process over hierarchical knowledge. HCAG adopts a two-phase design: an offline hierarchical abstraction phase that recursively parses code repositories and aligned theoretical texts to construct a multi-resolution semantic knowledge base explicitly linking theory, architecture, and implementation; and an online hierarchical retrieval and scaffolded generation phase that performs top-down, level-wise retrieval to guide LLMs in an architecture-then-module generation paradigm. To further improve robustness and consistency, HCAG integrates a multi-agent discussion inspired by cooperative game. We provide a theoretical analysis showing that hierarchical abstraction with adaptive node compression achieves cost-optimality compared to flat and iterative RAG baselines. Extensive experiments on diverse game-theoretic system generation tasks demonstrate that HCAG substantially outperforms representative repository-level methods in code quality, architectural coherence, and requirement pass rate. In addition, HCAG produces a large-scale, aligned theory-implementation dataset that effectively enhances domain-specific LLMs through post-training. Although demonstrated in AGT, HCAG paradigm also offers a general blueprint for mining, reusing, and generating complex systems from structured codebases in other domains.

</details>


### [65] [Procedural Refinement by LLM-driven Algorithmic Debugging for ARC-AGI-2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20334)
*Yu-Ning Qiu,Lin-Feng Zou,Jiong-Da Wang,Xue-Rong Yuan,Wang-Zhou Dai*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于神经-符号程序细化的方法ABPR，通过将大型语言模型与元解释器结合，并遵循算法程序调试的原则来提高复杂代码生成任务中的错误修复能力。实验结果表明，在Prolog这种当代大模型通常表现不佳的语言中，该方法能够实现56.67%的Pass@2得分，指出了将大型语言模型与经典形式化方法相结合以进行程序修复的一个更可审计的新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在复杂的代码生成任务中，基于对话的大规模语言模型（LLM）代码修复对于从初次编程错误中恢复的能力有限，因为这类代码修订主要依靠LLM的“合理推理”而非正式的、算法化的调试过程。然而，Udi Shapiro的算法程序调试(APD)理论为这样的调试提供了正式的基础，它将程序修复视为一个明确的、逐步的过程性精炼。

Method: 提出了Abduction-Based Procedural Refinement (ABPR)，一种神经-符号程序细化方法，该方法将LLM与一个元解释器结合起来，根据APD原则将程序执行具体化为紧凑的声明式树结构跟踪。选择Prolog作为目标语言，因为它具有适合于算法程序调试的声明式语义。

Result: ABPR与Gemini-3-Flash配对时，在ARC-AGI-2基准测试上实现了56.67%的Pass@2分数，即使是在现代LLM通常表现不佳的语言中也取得了这样的成绩。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，通过整合大型语言模型与经典形式化方法，可以朝着更加可审计的程序修复方向发展。

Abstract: In complex code-generation tasks, conversation-based LLM code repair exhibits limited ability to recover from first-pass programming errors, as such code  revisions are usually driven by LLMs' "plausible reasoning" rather than a formal, algorithmic debugging procedure. However, a formal foundation for such debugging exists in Udi Shapiro's theory of algorithmic program debugging (APD), which frames program repair as an explicit, stepwise procedural refinement process. In this paper, we propose a neuro-symbolic procedural refinement approach, Abduction-Based Procedural Refinement (ABPR), which couples an LLM with a meta-interpreter that materialises program execution into compact, declarative tree-structured traces, following the principles of APD. We evaluate ABPR on ARC-AGI-2, a benchmark requiring strong abstraction and debugging capabilities, and adopt Prolog as the target language due to its declarative semantics, which are well-suited to algorithmic program debugging. Our experiments show that ABPR paired with Gemini-3-Flash achieves a Pass@2 score of 56.67\% even in a language in which contemporary LLMs typically underperform. These results point towards a more auditable paradigm for program repair by integrating LLMs with classical formal methods.

### [66] [Beyond LLM-based test automation: A Zero-Cost Self-Healing Approach Using DOM Accessibility Tree Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20358)
*Renjith Nelson Joseph*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种无需成本的自愈测试自动化框架，该框架使用结构化的无障碍树提取算法来替代基于大型语言模型的元素发现方法。通过十级优先级定位器层次结构，从实时DOM中一次性获取强健的选择器，并在选择器失效时仅重新提取失效部分而非全部。经验证，该框架在不同设备和业务流程测试工作流中表现出色，实现了100%的通过率，且能快速自我修复失效选择器，适用于300多个测试案例而无需持续API费用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的网页测试自动化框架依赖于CSS选择器、XPath表达式和可见文本标签来定位UI元素，这些定位方式在网页应用更新其DOM结构或类名时容易变得脆弱，导致大规模测试失败。虽然有基于大型语言模型的自愈方法，但其每次运行产生的API成本对企业来说是不可接受的。因此，需要一种既有效又经济的解决方案来提高测试稳定性和降低维护成本。

Method: 提出了一种新的无成本自愈测试自动化框架，利用结构化无障碍树抽取算法代替昂贵的LLM为基础的方法进行元素查找。该框架定义了一个包含十个层级优先级的定位策略列表——按照W3C标准的角色获取(get_by_role)、data-testid属性、ARIA标签、CSS类片段以及可见文本等——用于从活跃DOM环境中单次遍历中生成稳定的定位符。此外，还引入了只针对故障定位符重新提取而非整个过程重做的自愈机制。

Result: 实验结果表明，在跨三个不同设备配置（桌面版Chrome、Safari及iPhone 15）与十个业务处理测试工作流下，此框架达到了31/31 (100%)的通过率，总执行时间为22秒（并行模式）。实际证明了其自愈能力：能在不到1秒内自动检测并重新发现陈旧的选择器，全程无需人工干预。该方案可扩展至超过300个测试用例，并且在整个过程中不产生任何额外的API调用开销。

Conclusion: 所提出的零成本自愈测试自动化框架成功解决了现有测试工具面临的主要挑战，即高维护成本与易碎性问题。通过采用创新性的定位策略与高效的自愈机制，不仅显著提高了测试效率与稳定性，同时也极大地降低了长期运营成本。

Abstract: Modern web test automation frameworks rely heavily on CSS selectors, XPath expressions, and visible text labels to locate UI elements. These locators are inherently brittle -- when web applications update their DOM structure or class names, test suites fail at scale. Existing self-healing approaches increasingly delegate element discovery to Large Language Models (LLMs), introducing per-run API costs that become prohibitive at enterprise scale. This paper presents a zero-cost self-healing test automation framework that replaces LLM-based discovery with a structured accessibility tree extraction algorithm. The framework employs a ten-tier priority-ranked locator hierarchy -- get_by_role (W3C standard), data-testid, ARIA labels, CSS class fragments, visible text -- to discover robust selectors from a live DOM in a single one-time pass. A self-healing mechanism re-extracts only broken selectors upon failure, rather than re-running full discovery. The framework is validated against automationexercise.com across three device profiles (Desktop Chrome, Desktop Safari, iPhone 15) and ten business process test workflows under a three-tier hierarchy (L0: Domain, L1: Process, L2: Feature). Results demonstrate a 31/31 (100%) pass rate across 31 test combinations with total execution time of 22 seconds under parallel execution. Self-healing is empirically demonstrated: a stale selector is detected and re-discovered in under 1 second with zero human intervention. The framework scales to 300+ test cases with zero ongoing API cost.

Additionally, the minimalist nature of current Python data visualization libraries tend to speed up the creation of images, disincentivizing users from spending time integrating additional tools into these short scripts. This paper proposes yProv4DV, a library lightweight designed to enable reproducible data visualization scripts through the use of provenance information, minimizing the necessity for code modifications. Through a single call, users can track inputs, outputs and source code files, enabling saving and full reproducibility of their data visualization software. As a result, this library fills a gap in reproducible research workflows by addressing the reproducibility of plots in scientific publications.

### [69] [Software Entropy: A Statistical Mechanics Framework for Software Testing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20528)
*Jerónimo Fotinós,Juan B. Cabral*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文基于统计力学提出了软件熵的正式定义，将测试套件视为对可能程序实现空间的宏观约束，并通过变异分析来近似局部可访问的微观状态空间，从而估计与熵相关的量。应用到实际项目中，展示了测试套件如何减少软件熵以及信息权重如何揭示单个测试在贡献上的结构差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量化软件熵的方法大多是启发式的，缺乏一个形式化的定义。本文旨在提供一种基于统计力学的软件熵定义方法，以便更准确地衡量软件系统的无序程度。

Method: 作者提出了一种新的软件熵度量方法，该方法视测试套件为可执行规范，即对可能程序实现空间施加的宏观限制。采用变异分析技术作为手段，来估算能够达到的局部微态空间，进而允许经验性地评估与熵有关的数量。

Result: 研究结果显示，所提出的指标能够定量测试套件是如何限制程序空间的，包括一个根据信息权重测量跨测试分布约束力的指标。当应用于真实世界项目时，发现测试套件确实减少了软件熵，并且信息权重揭示了单独测试之间在贡献上的结构性差异，这是传统代码覆盖率等指标无法捕捉到的信息。

Conclusion: 这项工作介绍了一种基于统计力学的形式化软件熵定义，提供了实用的熵相关数量估计方法。研究表明，新提出的熵度量不仅有助于理解测试套件如何影响软件系统组织结构，而且也指出了不同测试对于降低软件熵的具体贡献方式。

Abstract: The notion of software entropy is often invoked to describe the tendency of software systems to become increasingly disordered as they evolve, yet existing approaches to quantify it are largely heuristic. In this work we introduce a formal definition of software entropy grounded in statistical mechanics, interpreting test suites as executable specifications, that is, as macroscopic constraints on the space of possible program implementations. Within this framework, mutation analysis provides a practical approximation of the locally accessible microstate space, allowing entropy-related quantities to be estimated empirically. We propose metrics that quantify how test suites restrict program space, including an information-weighted measure of the distribution of constraint power across tests. Applying these ideas to a real-world project, we show how test suites reduce software entropy and how information weights reveal structural differences in the contribution of individual tests that traditional metrics such as code coverage fail to capture.

### [71] [LogFold: Compressing Logs with Structured Tokens and Hybrid Encoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20618)
*Shiwen Shan,Yintong Huo,Hongzhan Zhong,Zhining Wang,Yuxin Su,Zibin Zheng*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究发现结构化标记中的新冗余模式，并提出了一种新的类型感知编码策略来改进日志压缩。基于这一见解，我们引入了LogFold，这是一种新的日志压缩方法，它由四个组件构成：一个用于将标记分类为结构化、非结构化或静态类型的分析器；一个处理器，根据分隔符骨架在结构化标记中挖掘重复模式；一个针对不同类型标记定制数据表示的混合编码器；以及一个将输出压缩成存档文件的打包器。实验表明，LogFold在压缩比和速度上均优于现有技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着软件系统规模的增长，生成的日志数据量迅速增加，因此需要有效的压缩方法。虽然除了通用压缩工具（如Gzip, Bzip2）外，还有许多专为日志设计的压缩算法被开发出来，但它们由于忽视了某些复杂标记内的冗余性和缺乏针对多样化标记类型的精细编码策略而性能不佳。

Method: 本研究通过揭示结构化标记中的新冗余模式并提出一种新的类型感知编码策略来解决上述问题。基于这些发现，提出了LogFold方法，该方法包括四个主要部分：一个用于区分不同类型的令牌分析器；一个能基于分隔符框架从结构化令牌中提取重复模式的处理器；一个能够根据不同令牌类型调整其编码方式的混合编码器；以及最后负责将处理后的数据打包成档案文件的封装程序。

Result: 通过对16个公开日志数据集进行广泛的实验测试，结果显示LogFold相较于最先进的基准方案平均提高了11.11%的压缩比率，同时保持了9.842 MB/s的压缩速度。此外，消融研究表明每个组成部分的重要性，并且通过敏感性分析验证了LogFold在各种内部设置下的鲁棒性和稳定性。

Conclusion: LogFold是一种有效提高日志压缩效率的方法，它通过引入创新性的冗余识别与类型感知编码机制，在不牺牲处理速度的前提下显著提升了压缩率。

Abstract: Logs are essential for diagnosing failures and conducting retrospective studies, leading many software organizations to retain log messages for a long time. Nevertheless, the volume of generated log data grows rapidly as software systems grow, necessitating an effective compression method. Apart from general-purpose compressors (e.g., Gzip, Bzip2), many recent studies developed log-specific compression algorithms, but they offer suboptimal performance because of (1) overlooking redundancies within certain complex tokens, and (2) lacking a fine-grained encoding strategy for diverse token types.
  This work uncovers a new redundancy pattern in structured tokens and proposes a new type-aware encoding strategy to improve log compression. Building on this insight, we introduce LogFold, a novel log compression method consisting of four components: a token analyzer to classifies tokens as structured, unstructured, or static types; a processor that mines recurring patterns within structured tokens based on their delimiter skeletons; a hybrid encoder that tailors data representation according to token types; and a packer that compresses the output into an archive file. Extensive experiments on 16 public log datasets demonstrate that LogFold surpasses state-of-the-art baselines, achieving average compression ratio improvements by 11.11%, with a compression speed of 9.842 MB/s. Ablation studies further indicate the importance of each component. We also conduct sensitivity analyses to verify LogFold's robustness and stability across various internal settings.

### [72] [Evaluating LLM-generated code for domain-specific languages: molecular dynamics with LAMMPS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20630)

While their ability to generate general-purpose code is well established, their effectiveness in producing scientifically valid code/input scripting for domain-specific languages (DSLs) remains largely unexplored. We propose an evaluation procedure that enables domain experts (who may not be experts in the DSL) to assess the validity of LLM-generated input files for LAMMPS, a widely used molecular dynamics (MD) code, and to use those assessments to evaluate the performance of state-of-the-art LLMs and identify common issues. Key to the evaluation procedure are a normalization step to generate canonical files and an extensible parser for syntax analysis. The following steps isolate common errors without incurring costly tests (in time and computational resources). Once a working input file is generated, LLMs can accelerate verification tests. Our findings highlight limitations of LLMs in generating scientific DSLs and a practical path forward for their integration into domain-specific computational ecosystems by domain experts.

</details>


### [73] [Engineering Pitfalls in AI Coding Tools: An Empirical Study of Bugs in Claude Code, Codex, and Gemini CLI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20847)
*Ruixin Zhang,Wuyang Dai,Hung Viet Pham,Gias Uddin,Jinqiu Yang,Song Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究首次对构建AI辅助编码工具过程中遇到的工程陷阱进行了实证研究，通过分析Claude-Code、Codex和Gemini CLIs三个开源项目中超过3,800个公开报告的问题，发现功能相关问题占所有错误的67%以上，其中API、集成或配置错误是最常见的根本原因。

Conclusion: 通过对三个流行AI辅助编码工具中存在的大量bug进行细致分析，本文揭示了此类工具开发过程中常见的一些故障模式和重复出现的工程难题。研究结论为未来致力于打造更加可靠耐用的AI编程助手提供了重要的指导方向。

Abstract: The rapid integration of Large Language Models (LLMs) into software development workflows has given rise to a new class of AI-assisted coding tools, such as Claude-Code, Codex, and Gemini CLIs. While promising significant productivity gains, the engineering process of building these tools, which sit at the complex intersection of traditional software engineering, AI system design, and human-computer interaction, is fraught with unique and poorly understood challenges. This paper presents the first empirical study of engineering pitfalls in building such tools, on a systematic, manual analysis of over 3.8K publicly reported bugs in the open-source repositories of three AI-assisted coding tools (i.e., Claude-Code, Codex, and Gemini CLIs) on GitHub. Specifically, we employ an open-coding methodology to manually examine the issue description, associated user discussions, and developer responses. Through this process, we categorize each bug along multiple dimensions, including bug type, bug location, root cause, and observed symptoms. This fine-grained annotation enables us to characterize common failure patterns and identify recurring engineering challenges. Our results show that more than 67% of the bugs in these tools are related to functionality. In terms of root causes, 36.9% of the bugs stem from API, integration, or configuration errors. Consequently, the most commonly observed symptoms reported by users are API errors (18.3%), terminal problems (14%), and command failures (12.7%). These bugs predominantly affect the tool invocation (37.2%) and command execution (24.7%) stages of the system workflow. Collectively, our findings provide a critical roadmap for developers seeking to design the next generation of reliable and robust AI coding assistants.

We conducted a randomized controlled trial and built a dataset of 521 manual alert-removing interventions 2. We profiled intervention-like events using labeling functions. We built a dataset of 8,245 alert removals, more than 15 times larger than our dataset of manual interventions. We applied supervised learning to the alert removals, aiming to predict their impact on the tendency to bugs. Results: We identified complexity-reducing interventions that reduce the probability of future bugs. Such interventions are relevant to 33\% of Python files and might reduce the tendency to bugs by 5.5 percentage points. Conclusions: We presented methods to evaluate the impact of interventions. ### [78] [RuntimeSlicer: Towards Generalizable Unified Runtime State Representation for Failure Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21495)
*Lingzhe Zhang,Tong Jia,Weijie Hong,Mingyu Wang,Chiming Duan,Minghua He,Rongqian Wang,Xi Peng,Meiling Wang,Gong Zhang,Renhai Chen,Ying Li*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为RuntimeSlicer的统一运行时状态表示模型，旨在通过整合度量、跟踪和日志信息来改善故障管理的通用性。该方法包括统一运行时对比学习以及基于状态的任务导向调整策略，以支持轻量级任务模型的训练而无需重新设计特定模态的编码器或预处理流程。初步实验表明了其在系统状态建模和故障管理任务中的有效性和可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前软件系统的规模和复杂性不断增加，有效的故障管理变得至关重要但同时也更具挑战性。现有的故障管理方法通常依赖于面向任务的流水线，这导致了跨任务和系统之间的泛化能力有限。为了填补这一空白，需要一种能够统一处理不同数据源（如指标、追踪和日志）的方法，以提供更全面的系统运行时行为视图，并提高故障管理方案的通用性。

Method: 提出了RuntimeSlicer，一个朝向通用化故障管理的统一运行时状态表示模型。它通过直接编码指标、追踪和日志到单一的对齐系统状态嵌入中来捕获系统的整体运行时状况。为此引入了统一运行时对比学习技术，用于整合异构训练数据源并通过交叉模态对齐与时间一致性优化互补目标。此外，还提出了基于状态的任务导向调优方法，通过对运行时状态进行无监督划分并启用针对下游任务的状态条件适应。

Result: 初步实验显示，RuntimeSlicer在AIOps 2022数据集上展示了对于系统状态建模及故障管理任务的有效性和可行性。

Conclusion: RuntimeSlicer为解决大规模复杂软件系统中的故障管理问题提供了新的途径，通过创建统一的运行时表示模型增强了跨任务和系统的泛化能力，同时简化了针对特定任务的模型训练过程。

Abstract: Modern software systems operate at unprecedented scale and complexity, where effective failure management is critical yet increasingly challenging. Metrics, traces, and logs provide complementary views of system runtime behavior, but existing failure management approaches typically rely on task-oriented pipelines that tightly couple modality-specific preprocessing, representation learning, and downstream models, resulting in limited generalization across tasks and systems. To fill this gap, we propose RuntimeSlicer, a unified runtime state representation model towards generalizable failure management. RuntimeSlicer pre-trains a task-agnostic representation model that directly encodes metrics, traces, and logs into a single, aligned system-state embedding capturing the holistic runtime condition of the system. To train RuntimeSlicer, we introduce Unified Runtime Contrastive Learning, which integrates heterogeneous training data sources and optimizes complementary objectives for cross-modality alignment and temporal consistency. Building upon the learned system-state embeddings, we further propose State-Aware Task-Oriented Tuning, which performs unsupervised partitioning of runtime states and enables state-conditioned adaptation for downstream tasks. This design allows lightweight task-oriented models to be trained on top of the unified embedding without redesigning modality-specific encoders or preprocessing pipelines. Preliminary experiments on the AIOps 2022 dataset demonstrate the feasibility and effectiveness of RuntimeSlicer for system state modeling and failure management tasks.

</details>


### [79] [LLM-Based Test Case Generation in DBMS through Monte Carlo Tree Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21530)
*Yujia Chen,Yingli Zhou,Fangyuan Zhang,Cuiyun Gao*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: MIST, a framework that uses LLMs and Monte Carlo Tree Search to generate SQL test cases for DBMSs, improves coverage metrics significantly over baseline approaches.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To overcome the challenges faced by lightweight LLMs in generating high-quality, diverse, and syntactically valid SQL queries for proprietary dialects of DBMSs, as well as to enhance code coverage beyond a shallow level.

Method: Proposed MIST, which integrates Feature-Guided Error-Driven Test Case Synthetization for producing valid and diverse SQL queries, and Monte Carlo Tree Search-Based Test Case Mutation for optimizing seed query selection and mutation rule application to explore deeper execution paths.

Result: MIST demonstrated significant improvements in line, function, and branch coverage across three widely-used DBMSs with four lightweight LLMs, outperforming the baseline approach.

Conclusion: MIST effectively addresses the limitations of LLMs in SQL test case generation for DBMSs, leading to enhanced system reliability through improved code coverage and query diversity.

Abstract: Database Management Systems (DBMSs) are fundamental infrastructure for modern data-driven applications, where thorough testing with high-quality SQL test cases is essential for ensuring system reliability. Traditional approaches such as fuzzing can be effective for specific DBMSs, but adapting them to different proprietary dialects requires substantial manual effort. Large Language Models (LLMs) present promising opportunities for automated SQL test generation, but face critical challenges in industrial environments. First, lightweight models are widely used in organizations due to security and privacy constraints, but they struggle to generate syntactically valid queries for proprietary SQL dialects. Second, LLM-generated queries are often semantically similar and exercise only shallow execution paths, thereby quickly reaching a coverage plateau. To address these challenges, we propose MIST, an LLM-based test case generatIon framework for DBMS through Monte Carlo Tree search. MIST consists of two stages: Feature-Guided Error-Driven Test Case Synthetization, which constructs a hierarchical feature tree and uses error feedback to guide LLM generation, aiming to produce syntactically valid and semantically diverse queries for different DBMS dialects, and Monte Carlo Tree Search-Based Test Case Mutation, which jointly optimizes seed query selection and mutation rule application guided by coverage feedback, aiming at boosting code coverage by exploring deeper execution paths. Experiments on three widely-used DBMSs with four lightweight LLMs show that MIST achieves average improvements of 43.3% in line coverage, 32.3% in function coverage, and 46.4% in branch coverage compared to the baseline approach with the highest line coverage of 69.3% in the Optimizer module.

</details>

Motivation: 随着软件开发中对能效关注的增加，需要有能够测量能耗的工具。尽管已有若干开源项目提供了能源测量工具，但它们的特点和采用情况仍待进一步探索。

Method: 采用挖掘软件仓库（MSR）的方法来识别、分类并分析GitHub上公开可用的软件能源监控工具。通过定性分析初步数据集中的585个仓库，确定了关键设计方面，包括测量粒度和基础设计原则。

Result: 在对最初的数据集进行了深入分析之后，研究人员保留了24个与能源测量相关的软件工具仓库。研究揭示了这类工具从最初的以CPU为中心和机器级别的监控工具逐渐发展为支持更广泛层级（如进程级、容器级以及AI工作负载级别）且具备排放估计功能的多样化工具的趋势。

Conclusion: 这项研究首次从MSR的角度提供了一个关于开源能源与排放测量工具结构化的概览，这可能有助于软件架构师在设计节能型软件时做出决策。

Abstract: Energy efficiency has become a growing concern in software development, leading to the need for tools designed to measure energy consumption. While several energy measurement tools are available as open-source projects, their characteristics and adoption remain underexplored. This work presents an empirical study based on a Mining Software Repositories (MSR) approach to identify, classify, and analyze software energy monitoring tools publicly available on GitHub. We qualitatively analyzed an initial dataset of 585 repositories to identify key design aspects, including measurement granularity and underlying design principles. After this analysis, we retained 24 repositories as relevant energy measuring software tools. The qualitative analysis we conduct reveals a clear evolution from early CPU-centric and machine-level monitoring utilities toward more diverse tools that support multi-level granularity (process, container, and AI workload levels) and integrate emission estimation capabilities. This study provides the first structured overview of open-source energy and emission measurement tools from an MSR perspective, which may be beneficial for software architects when designing energy-aware software.

</details>


### [82] [StreamSampling.jl: Efficient Sampling from Data Streams in Julia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21996)
*Adriano Meligrana*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: StreamSampling.jl是一个Julia库，它提供了一种从数据流中进行单次遍历采样的高效方法，无需事先知道数据项总数。该库保持了小而恒定的内存占用，并且避免了将整个数据流加载到内存中的需要。通过实证基准测试表明，在性能和内存使用方面优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发StreamSampling.jl是为了克服在处理未知长度的数据流时遇到的问题，比如需要较大的内存来存储全部或部分数据流。这个库旨在提供一种更加通用且高效的解决方案，以支持即使是在资源受限环境下的在线采样。

Method: 通过利用Julia语言的特点，StreamSampling.jl实现了几种在线抽样算法，这些算法能够在只访问每个元素一次的情况下完成采样过程。关键在于维护一个固定大小的样本集，随着新元素的到来动态更新此集合。

Result: 实证研究表明，与传统的完全加载数据然后进行采样的方法相比，StreamSampling.jl不仅减少了内存消耗，还提高了处理速度。这使得它成为处理大规模数据集的理想选择。

Conclusion: StreamSampling.jl为处理未知长度的数据流提供了一个有效率、低内存使用的解决方案，适合于大数据应用场合。此外，它提供的灵活性使其能够适应多种不同的应用场景。

Abstract: StreamSampling$.$jl is a Julia library designed to provide general and efficient methods for sampling from data streams in a single pass, even when the total number of items is unknown. In this paper, we describe the capabilities of the library and its advantages over traditional sampling procedures, such as maintaining a small, constant memory footprint and avoiding the need to fully materialize the stream in memory. Furthermore, we provide empirical benchmarks comparing online sampling methods against standard approaches, demonstrating performance and memory improvements.

*Margaret-Anne Storey*

Main category: cs.SE

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 为了维持软件系统的长期健康，需要对技术债务、认知债务和意图债务给予足够的重视，并采取措施管理它们。

Abstract: Over time, the shared understanding that makes a software system safe to change quietly erodes. This gradual loss of understanding across a team increases cognitive debt, while the loss of captured rationale leads to intent debt. These may become more important, than technical debt in AI-assisted software development. This article proposes a triple debt model to reason about software health. It is built around three interacting debt types: technical debt in code, cognitive debt in people, and intent debt in externalized knowledge. Cognitive debt concerns what people understand; intent debt concerns what is explicitly captured for both people and machines to use in the future.

### [84] [DGNNFlow: A Streaming Dataflow Architecture for Real-Time Edge-based Dynamic GNN Inference in HL-LHC Trigger Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20364)
*Davendra Maharaj,Tu Pham,Peter Meiring,Kyungmin Park,Sena Durgut,Cong Hao,Matteo Cremonesi*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出了DGNNFlow，一种用于实时基于边的动态GNN推理应用的数据流架构，特别适用于HL-LHC触发系统。该架构通过硬件支持动态计算边嵌入、解决数据依赖性问题以及执行输入动态图构建辅助设置来实现高效推理。相比GPU和CPU，在不同批量大小下均实现了显著的速度提升和更低的能耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来高能物理实验将产生比现有量多10倍的碰撞数据，但离线计算能力和存储有限，需要依靠FPGA运行超低延迟机器学习模型来进行在线过滤有用事件，同时保持低功耗。现有的GNN加速器基于静态图结构设计，这在实时HL-LHC触发系统中不适用，因为这些系统中的边嵌入会根据邻居节点嵌入实时变化。

Method: 开发了名为DGNNFlow的新颖数据流架构，它具有三项关键贡献：一是提供硬件支持以动态计算边嵌入；二是解决了基于边的动态GNN数据流中的数据依赖性问题；三是进行输入动态图构造辅助设置，完全支持没有预定义边嵌入的模型。使用AMD Alveo U50 FPGA部署了DGNNFlow，并在200 MHz时钟频率下评估了端到端延迟。

Result: 与NVIDIA RTX A6000 GPU相比，当批量大小从1到4时，DGNNFlow实现了1.6倍至6.3倍的速度提升及仅为前者的0.22倍功耗；而与Intel Xeon Gold 6226R CPU相比，则分别达到了3.2倍至5.1倍的速度提升及0.25倍功耗。

Conclusion: DGNNFlow为实时处理HL-LHC触发系统等场景下的动态GNN推理提供了有效解决方案，不仅提高了处理速度还降低了能耗，显示出其在高能物理实验及其他相关领域应用的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Dynamic GNN inference has exhibited effectiveness in High Energy Physics (HEP) experiments at High Luminosity Large Hadron Collider (HL-LHC) due to strong capability to model complex particle interactions in collision events. Future HEP experiments will involve detectors that produce 10x more collision data to help unlocking physics discoveries. Due to limitations in offline compute capacity and storage, revamped trigger systems require FPGAs to run ultra-low-latency Machine Learning models for online filtering of useful events with low power consumption. State-of-the-art GNN accelerators relied on static graph structures, but this assumption breaks down in real-time HL-LHC trigger systems and edge-based dynamic GNN models where edge embeddings change in-place based on neighbor node embeddings at runtime. We propose DGNNFlow, a novel dataflow architecture for real-time edge-based dynamic GNN inference applications, especially HL-LHC trigger systems, with three key contributions. First, we introduce hardware support for dynamic computation of edge embeddings. Second, we resolve data dependencies in edge-based dynamic GNN dataflow, where edge embedding is formulated using its source and target nodes. Third, we perform input dynamic graph construction auxiliary setup for complete support of models without pre-defined edge embeddings. We deployed DGNNFlow using AMD Alveo U50 FPGA to evaluate end-to-end latency on-board at 200 MHz clock frequency. DGNNFlow achieved 1.6x-6.3x speedup and 0.22x power consumption compared to GPU (NVIDIA RTX A6000) with batch sizes from 1 to 4, 3.2x-5.1x speedup and 0.25x power consumption compared to CPU (Intel Xeon Gold 6226R). Our complete implementation is publicly available on GitHub.

</details>


### [85] [SkyHOST: A Unified Architecture for Cross-Cloud Hybrid Object and Stream Transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20512)
*Muhammad Arslan Tariq,Grégoire Danoy,Pascal Bouvry*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: SkyHOST is a unified data movement architecture that bridges the gap between bulk object transfer and streaming workloads, providing operational simplicity and competitive throughput for cross-region transfers.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation behind this paper is to address the limitations of traditional transfer tools, which are specialized for either stream replication or bulk transfer, leading to the need for users to manage multiple systems. SkyHOST aims to provide a single control plane and CLI to handle both types of data movement, thereby simplifying operations and supporting rapid decision-making and analytics across multiple cloud providers and regions.

Method: SkyHOST (Hybrid Object and Stream Transfer) is built upon the Skyplane framework. It supports URI-based routing to automatically choose the right transfer mechanism, catering to both structured data and large binary objects. The system is designed to unify the management of different data movement patterns under one control plane, making it easier for users to handle diverse data transfer needs without having to deploy separate systems.

Result: Through an environmental monitoring use case and empirical evaluation, the authors demonstrate that SkyHOST successfully consolidates heterogeneous data movement patterns into a single control plane, achieving competitive throughput in cross-region data transfers. This not only simplifies the operational complexity but also maintains high performance.

Conclusion: SkyHOST presents a solution for managing both bulk object transfers and streaming workloads through a unified interface, offering a more efficient and simpler approach to data movement across various cloud environments and regions. Its ability to automatically select the appropriate transfer mechanism based on the type of data being moved makes it a versatile tool for modern cloud and big data applications.

Abstract: Cloud and big data workloads are increasingly distributing data across multiple cloud providers and regions for rapid decision-making and analytics. Traditional transfer tools are typically specialized for a single paradigm, either stream replication or bulk transfer. This specialization forces users to deploy and manage separate systems with different configurations for each transfer pattern. This paper presents SkyHOST (Hybrid Object and Stream Transfer), a unified data movement architecture built upon the Skyplane framework to bridge the gap between bulk object transfer and streaming workloads through a single control plane and CLI. SkyHOST manages URI-based routing to automatically select the appropriate transfer mechanism, supporting both structured data for record-level ingestion and chunk-based transfer for large binary objects. We demonstrate, through an environmental monitoring use case and empirical evaluation, that SkyHOST provides operational simplicity by consolidating heterogeneous data movement patterns under a single control plane while achieving competitive throughput for cross-region transfers.

### [86] [Epistemic Observability in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20531)
*Tony Mason*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 该论文发现模型在编造内容时报告的置信度最高，并且自我报告的置信度与准确性呈负相关。研究证明，仅通过文本观察无法可靠地区分诚实的模型输出和看似合理的捏造。为了解决这个问题，研究人员构建了一个张量接口，通过导出计算副产品（每个令牌的熵和对数概率分布）来提高检测准确性。这种方法优于所有基于文本的基线方法，并提供了一种实用的方法来决定如何分配验证资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于解决一个关键问题：当模型生成内容时，它们报告的置信度与其实际准确性之间的关系是相反的。此外，在仅有文本输出的情况下，监督者很难区分模型的真实答案和虚构的答案。这导致了对于如何有效监测和确保AI系统诚实性的挑战。

Method: 研究采用了四个不同的模型家族进行实验，并提出了一个形式化的假设框架来分析这一现象。同时，为了克服仅基于文本观察带来的局限性，研究者设计了一个能够导出与标准训练下正确性结构耦合的计算副产品（如每个令牌的熵值等）的张量接口。

Result: 结果表明，通过使用提出的张量接口以及利用每个令牌的熵值作为信号，可以显著提升识别模型生成内容真实性的能力。在不同预算水平下测试时，此方法比所有基于纯文本的方法表现更好。此外，还提供了一份成本曲面图，帮助系统构建者根据验证预算做出决策。

Conclusion: 结论指出，要准确地监控并保证AI系统的诚实行为，需要超越单纯依赖文本信息的传统做法。本研究提出的方法不仅理论上可行，而且在实践中也显示出了优越性能，为未来开发更加可靠的人工智能应用提供了新的思路。

Abstract: We find that models report highest confidence precisely when they are fabricating. Across four model families (OLMo-3, Llama-3.1, Qwen3, Mistral), self-reported confidence inversely correlates with accuracy, with AUC ranging from 0.28 to 0.36 where 0.5 is random guessing.
  We prove, under explicit formal assumptions, that this is not a capability gap but an observational one. Under text-only observation, where a supervisor sees only the model's output text, no monitoring system can reliably distinguish honest model outputs from plausible fabrications. We prove two results: first, that any policy conditioning only on the query cannot satisfy epistemic honesty across ambiguous world states; second, that no learning algorithm optimizing reward from a text-only supervisor can converge to honest behavior when the supervisor's observations are identical for both grounded and fabricated responses. Within our formal model, these impossibilities hold regardless of model scale or training procedure, including RLHF and instruction tuning.
  We construct a tensor interface that escapes the impossibility by exporting computational byproducts (per-token entropy and log-probability distributions) that are structurally coupled to correctness under standard training. Per-token entropy achieves pooled AUC 0.757, outperforming all text baselines by 2.5--3.9 percentage points at every budget level tested (10\%, 20\%, 30\%). The entropy signal generalizes across architectures (Spearman $ρ= 0.762$).
  The core contribution is a cost surface where the empirical mapping from verification budget (fraction of queries receiving expensive checks) to detection accuracy for each judge strategy is a practical lookup for system builders deciding how to allocate verification resources. The contribution is the map. The territory is the system you are building.

</details>


### [87] [Modernizing Amdahl's Law: How AI Scaling Laws Shape Computer Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20654)
*Chien-Ping Lu*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 该论文重新定义了适用于现代异构系统和可扩展工作负载的Amdahl定律，揭示了一个有限崩溃阈值：当可扩展部分超过某一临界值时，即使专用硬件相比可编程计算有任何效率优势，专业化也会变得不再最优，并且对最佳专业投资会降至零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的Amdahl定律假设串行与并行工作之间存在固定分解及同质复制，但在现代系统中，这种设定已不足以描述结合了专门加速器、可编程计算、张量数据路径以及不断发展的流水线的实际情况。文章旨在解决资源在异构硬件上的分配问题，同时考虑了不同硬件效率差异以及工作负载结构如何影响额外计算转化为价值的有效性。

Method: 通过重新定义Amdahl定律来适应当前复杂多变的计算环境，特别是针对那些具有可扩展工作负载特性的现代异构系统。

Result: 研究发现了一个关键点——即有限崩溃阈值的存在：一旦可扩展的工作比例超过了特定临界值，则无论专用硬件相对于通用计算有何种效率优势，继续追求更高程度的专业化都不再是最优选择。此外，对于专用硬件的最佳投资额将降为零。

Conclusion: 随着GPU可编程性的增加以及为什么领域特定的人工智能加速器未能取代GPU的现象，可以通过新框架得到解释。这表明，在达到某个临界点后，尽管专用硬件可能更有效率，但其投资回报率下降，导致转向更加灵活的解决方案成为趋势。

Abstract: Classical Amdahl's Law assumes a fixed decomposition between serial and parallel work and homogeneous replication; historically, it bounds how much parallel speedup is attainable. Modern systems instead combine specialized accelerators with programmable compute, tensor datapaths, and evolving pipelines, while empirical scaling laws shift which stages absorb marginal compute. The central tension is therefore not the serial-versus-parallel split alone, but resource allocation across heterogeneous hardware, given efficiency differences, and workload structures that determine how effectively additional compute can be converted into value. We reformulate Amdahl's Law for modern heterogeneous systems with scalable workloads. The analysis yields a finite collapse threshold: beyond a critical scalable fraction, specialization becomes suboptimal for any efficiency advantage of specialized hardware over programmable compute, and optimal specialized investment falls to zero, a phase transition rather than an asymptotic tail. We use this framework to interpret increasing GPU programmability and why domain-specific AI accelerators have not displaced GPUs.

</details>


### [88] [WWW.Serve: Interconnecting Global LLM Services through Decentralization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20661)
*Huanyu Wang,Ziyu Xia,Zhuoming Chen,Beidi Chen*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为WWW.Serve的去中心化框架，旨在解决大型语言模型服务的可扩展性瓶颈问题。该框架允许参与者灵活决定参与策略和资源承诺，并支持自我组织请求调度，从而在没有集中协调的情况下自动分配请求。实验证明，WWW.Serve可以提高全球服务水平目标达成率至1.5倍，并减少27.6%的延迟时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型（LLM）服务主要采用中心化模式，这导致了可扩展性的瓶颈以及大量分散GPU资源的利用不足。虽然去中心化提供了一个有希望的选择，但现有框架往往只关注于GPU提供商之间的合作而忽视了它们之间固有的竞争动态，施加了很多限制条件。

Method: 提出了一个名为WWW.Serve的新框架，这是一个用于连接全球LLM服务的去中心化框架。它允许参与者灵活地确定自己的参与政策与资源投入，并且支持自组织式的请求分发机制。

Result: 实验结果表明，WWW.Serve能够将全球SLO（服务级别目标）达成率提高多达1.5倍，并降低27.6%的延迟。其性能接近甚至有时超过中心化调度的效果，同时完全保留了去中心化带来的好处。

Conclusion: WWW.Serve作为真实世界中去中心化LLM服务的一个有前途的基础展现出了巨大潜力。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) services are mostly centralized, leading to scalability bottlenecks and underutilization of substantial scattered GPU resources. While decentralization offers a promising alternative, existing frameworks primarily focus on cooperation among GPU providers while overlooking their inherent competitive dynamics, imposing substantial constraints such as excessive platform-level oversight or rigid requirements to execute all assigned requests using fixed software stacks on fixed hardware configurations. We argue that such assumptions are unrealistic in real-world decentralized environments. To this end, we propose WWW.Serve, a decentralized framework for interconnecting LLM services worldwide. It allows participants to flexibly determine their participation policies and resource commitments, and supports self-organizing request dispatch, enabling the network to autonomously allocate requests without centralized coordination. Empirically, we show that WWW.Serve improves global SLO (service-level-objective) attainment by up to 1.5x and lowers latency by 27.6%. Its performance approaches, and in some cases surpasses, centralized scheduling, while fully preserving the benefits of decentralization. These results highlight WWW.Serve as a promising foundation for real-world, decentralized LLM serving.

</details>


### [89] [Compass: Optimizing Compound AI Workflows for Dynamic Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20821)
*Milos Gravara,Juan Luis Herrera,Stefan Nastic*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Compass的新框架，该框架通过离线优化和在线适应实现动态配置切换，从而在复合AI系统中根据当前负载情况在精度和延迟之间进行权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复合AI系统需要在不同负载条件下满足准确性、延迟和成本目标。然而，许多部署运行在固定基础设施上，无法进行水平扩展。现有的方法只针对准确性进行优化，并未考虑工作负载条件的变化。作者观察到，复合AI系统可以通过切换配置来适应基础设施容量，基于当前负载情况在准确性和延迟之间进行权衡。

Method: Compass框架由三个组件组成：用于配置发现的COMPASS-V算法、用于切换策略推导的Planner以及用于运行时适应的Elastico Controller。COMPASS-V使用有限差分引导搜索及爬山与横向扩展相结合的方法发现精确可行的配置。Planner则对这些配置在目标硬件上进行性能分析，并利用基于排队论模型的方法来推导出切换策略。Elastico负责监控队列深度，并依据所设定阈值来进行配置切换。

Result: 对于两种不同的复合AI工作流，COMPASS-V相比详尽搜索平均减少了57.5%的配置评估次数，在严格的准确性阈值下效率提高了95.3%。运行时适应机制在动态负载模式下实现了90-98%的服务水平目标（SLO）合规性，比静态高精度基线提高了71.6%的SLO合规性，同时相对于静态快速基线提升了3-5%的准确性。

Conclusion: Compass框架有效地解决了复合AI系统在固定基础设施上的动态配置问题，能够在保持高水平服务的同时显著提升系统的灵活性和资源利用率。

Abstract: Compound AI is a distributed intelligence approach that represents a unified system orchestrating specialized AI/ML models with engineered software components into AI workflows. Compound AI production deployments must satisfy accuracy, latency, and cost objectives under varying loads. However, many deployments operate on fixed infrastructure where horizontal scaling is not viable. Existing approaches optimize solely for accuracy and do not consider changes in workload conditions. We observe that compound AI systems can switch between configurations to fit infrastructure capacity, trading accuracy for latency based on current load. This requires discovering multiple Pareto-optimal configurations from a combinatorial search space and determining when to switch between them at runtime. We present Compass, a novel framework that enables dynamic configuration switching through offline optimization and online adaptation. Compass consists of three components: COMPASS-V algorithm for configuration discovery, Planner for switching policy derivation, and Elastico Controller for runtime adaptation. COMPASS-V discovers accuracy-feasible configurations using finite-difference guided search and a combination of hill-climbing and lateral expansion. Planner profiles these configurations on target hardware and derives switching policies using a queuing theory based model. Elastico monitors queue depth and switches configurations based on derived thresholds. Across two compound AI workflows, COMPASS-V achieves 100% recall while reducing configuration evaluations by 57.5% on average compared to exhaustive search, with efficiency gains reaching 95.3% at tight accuracy thresholds. Runtime adaptation achieves 90-98% SLO compliance under dynamic load patterns, improving SLO compliance by 71.6% over static high-accuracy baselines, while simultaneously improving accuracy by 3-5% over static fast baselines.

</details>


### [90] [Communication Lower Bounds and Algorithms for Sketching with Random Dense Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20966)
*Hussam Al Daas,Grey Ballard,Laura Grigori,Md Taufique Hussain,Suraj Kumar,Mohammad Marufur Rahman,Kathryn Rouse*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在分布式内存算法中进行草图绘制的通信下界，并提出了接近这些下界的最优通信算法。此外，还扩展了方法来确定Nyström近似计算中的通信下界，并展示了所提算法在现代超级计算机基础设施上的并行可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管草图绘制技术在机器学习应用中变得越来越重要，但针对大规模矩阵的草图绘制往往需要分布式内存算法，在这种情况下，现代超级计算集群上的通信开销成为了一个关键瓶颈。因此，研究如何减少通信成本对于提高此类算法效率至关重要。

Method: 通过建立使用密集矩阵进行草图绘制时的通信下界，分析了执行并行草图绘制所需的数据移动量。基于这些下界设计了通信最优算法，并进一步扩展到Nyström近似中的两次草图绘制情况。开发了新的并行算法，其通信成本接近于理论下界。

Result: 研究表明，当处理器数量较少时不需要任何通信；为达到通信最优而提出的新算法被证明是有效的。此外，新算法在包括CPU和GPU在内的最新超级计算平台上实现了良好的并行扩展性。

Conclusion: 这项工作不仅为理解草图绘制操作的内在通信需求提供了基础，而且通过提出几乎达到通信下界的高效算法，为实际应用提供了解决方案。

Abstract: Sketching is widely used in randomized linear algebra for low-rank matrix approximation, column subset selection, and many other problems, and it has gained significant traction in machine learning applications. However, sketching large matrices often necessitates distributed memory algorithms, where communication overhead becomes a critical bottleneck on modern supercomputing clusters. Despite its growing relevance, distributed-memory parallel strategies for sketching remain largely unexplored. In this work, we establish communication lower bounds for sketching using dense matrices that determine how much data movement is required to perform it in parallel. One important observation of our lower bounds is that no communication is required for a small number of processors. We show that our lower bounds are tight by presenting communication optimal algorithms. Furthermore, we extend our approach to determine communication lower bounds for computations of Nyström approximation where sketching is applied twice. We also introduce novel parallel algorithms whose communication costs are close to the lower bounds. Finally, we implement our algorithms on modern state-of-the-art supercomputing infrastructures which have both CPU- and GPU-equipped systems and demonstrate their parallel scalability.

### [91] [NeSy-Edge: Neuro-Symbolic Trustworthy Self-Healing in the Computing Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21145)
*Peihan Ye,Alfreds Lapkovskis,Alaa Saleh,Qiyang Zhang,Praveen Kumar Donta*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出NeSy-Edge框架，一种针对计算连续体中的可信自我修复的神经符号框架，能够在资源受限的边缘设备上实现鲁棒的故障管理。实验表明，即使在高噪声水平下，NeSy-Edge也能达到高达75%的根本原因分析准确率和65%的端到端准确率，同时仅使用约1500MB本地内存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着现代AI服务的计算需求不断增长，执行环境正从集中的云扩展到跨越边缘和终端设备的计算连续体。然而，这些环境的大规模、异构性以及跨层依赖性使得保持韧性变得困难。现有的故障管理方法往往过于静态、碎片化或过重，难以支持及时的自愈，特别是在日志噪音大和边缘资源受限的情况下。

Method: 提出了NeSy-Edge，这是一个用于计算连续体中可信自我修复的神经符号框架。该框架采用“边缘优先”的设计理念，在资源受限的边缘节点上进行本地感知与推理，而云端模型仅在最终诊断阶段被调用。具体来说，NeSy-Edge将原始运行时日志转换为结构化的事件表示，构建一个先验约束稀疏符号因果图，并结合因果证据与历史故障排除知识来进行根本原因分析及恢复建议。

Result: 通过代表性Loghub数据集在多个语义噪声级别下的评估显示，NeSy-Edge即便在最高噪声水平下也能够保持稳健，实现了高达75%的根本原因分析准确性以及65%的端到端准确性，同时仅需大约1500MB的本地内存即可运行。

Conclusion: NeSy-Edge提供了一种有效的方法来提高边缘计算环境中系统的韧性和可靠性，特别是在面对资源限制和高噪声数据时。

Abstract: The computational demands of modern AI services are increasingly shifting execution beyond centralized clouds toward a computing continuum spanning edge and end devices. However, the scale, heterogeneity, and cross-layer dependencies of these environments make resilience difficult to maintain. Existing fault-management methods are often too static, fragmented, or heavy to support timely self-healing, especially under noisy logs and edge resource constraints. To address these limitations, this paper presents NeSy-Edge, a neuro-symbolic framework for trustworthy self-healing in the computing continuum. The framework follows an edge-first design, where a resource-constrained edge node performs local perception and reasoning, while a cloud model is invoked only at the final diagnosis stage. Specifically, NeSy-Edge converts raw runtime logs into structured event representations, builds a prior-constrained sparse symbolic causal graph, and integrates causal evidence with historical troubleshooting knowledge for root-cause analysis and recovery recommendation. We evaluate our work on representative Loghub datasets under multiple levels of semantic noise, considering parsing quality, causal reasoning, end-to-end diagnosis, and edge-side resource usage. The results show that NeSy-Edge remains robust even at the highest noise level, achieving up to 75% root-cause analysis accuracy and 65% end-to-end accuracy while operating within about 1500 MB of local memory.

</details>


### [92] [Decidability of Livelock Detection for Parameterized Self-Disabling Unidirectional Rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21443)
*Aly Farahat*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本研究证明了对于具有有界域$\mathbb{Z}_m$的参数化对称单向自禁用进程环，死锁检测在多项式时间内是可判定的。给定由局部转换集$T$指定的协议，算法能够决定是否存在某个环大小$K\geq2$下的死锁，并且运行时间与$K$无关为$O(|T|^3)$。该算法计算有限集$T$上一个通缩单调算子的最大不动点，并据此判断是否存在死锁。此外，还处理了$(1,1)$-非对称情况，其中有一个特殊进程$P_0$与其他$K-1$个相同进程不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于解决参数化系统中特定类型的死锁问题，特别是针对对称单向自禁用进程环以及一种特殊情况下的非对称环。通过提供一个有效的算法来判定这类系统的死锁状态，无需遍历所有可能的环尺寸即可确定整个系统是否自由于死锁。

Method: 采用基于Farahat之前工作中的代数特征描述方法，但进一步解决了可判定性问题。算法核心在于寻找定义在局部转换集合$T$上的最大不动点，这代表了能够维持每个进程中伪死锁的最大转换集合。如果此不动点为空，则表明对于所有环大小$K$来说系统都是无死锁的。

Result: 成功开发出了一种可在多项式时间内（具体为$O(|T|^3)$）内完成的算法，用于检测参数化对称单向自禁用进程环及$(1,1)$-非对称情形下的死锁存在性。该算法不依赖于具体的环大小$K$值，因此极大地提高了效率。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，通过应用代数方法可以有效地解决一类重要参数化系统中的死锁检测问题，不仅提供了理论基础同时也给出了实用性强的具体实现方案。

Abstract: We prove that livelock detection is \emph{decidable in polynomial time} for parameterized symmetric unidirectional rings of self-disabling processes with bounded domain $\mathbb{Z}_m$. Given a protocol specified by its set of local transitions $T$, the algorithm decides whether a livelock exists for \emph{some} ring size $K\!\geq\!2$, running in $O(|T|^3)$ time independent of $K$. The algorithm computes the greatest fixed point of a deflationary monotone operator on the finite set $T$ and returns \emph{livelock} iff the fixed point is non-empty. The livelock freedom argument rests on maximality: the fix-point is the largest set of transitions that can together sustain a pseudolivelock at every process; its emptiness certifies freedom for all $K$ without any search over ring sizes. The work is grounded in the algebraic characterization of livelocks from Farahat~\citep{farahat2012}, which establishes necessary and sufficient conditions for livelock existence but does not address decidability. We also handle the $(1,1)$-asymmetric case in which one distinguished process $P_0$ differs from the remaining $K\!-\!1$ identical processes. Code and algebraic foundation are at the URL: https://github.com/cosmoparadox/mathematical-tools.

</details>


### [93] [Communication-Avoiding SpGEMM via Trident Partitioning on Hierarchical GPU Interconnects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21444)
*Julian Bellavita,Lorenzo Pichetti,Thomas Pasquali,Flavio Vella,Giulia Guidi*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Trident的分布式稀疏矩阵乘法算法，该算法通过避免通信技术和异步通信来利用现代超级计算机互连的层次结构和异构架构。Trident在处理非结构化稀疏矩阵时表现优异，与2D SpGEMM相比速度提高了1.54倍至2.38倍，并减少了节点间通信量达两倍。此外，Trident还被证明能够加速马尔可夫聚类过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于稀疏性通常是高度非结构化的，在科学计算和大规模数据分析中，两个稀疏矩阵相乘（SpGEMM）这一关键内核实现高性能面临挑战。这限制了内存效率和可扩展性。在分布式内存环境下，跨节点交换和合并部分乘积的成本进一步限制了性能。这些问题在具有深层、层次化GPU互连的现代异构超级计算机上更加严重。当前的SpGEMM实现忽略了节点内部和节点之间带宽之间的差距，导致不必要的数据移动和同步，未能充分利用快速的节点内部互连。

Method: 为了解决上述问题，研究者们提出了Trident，这是一种层次感知的2D分布式SpGEMM算法，它使用了避免通信的技术和异步通信来利用现代超级计算机互连的层次性和异构性。Trident的核心是新颖的三叉分区方案，该方案使得层次感知分解成为可能，并通过利用节点内GPU之间相比于节点间的更高带宽来减少节点间通信。

Result: Trident对非结构化矩阵进行了评估，相较于普通的2D SpGEMM实现了最高2.38倍的速度提升，对应的几何平均提速为1.54倍。Trident能够在NERSC的Perlmutter超级计算机上将节点间通信量降低最多两倍。另外，实验表明Trident能够有效加速Markov Clustering，相较于竞争策略可以达到高达2倍的速度提升。

Conclusion: Trident算法通过优化通信模式和利用异构系统中的层次结构，成功地提升了分布式稀疏矩阵乘法的性能。这对于需要执行大量稀疏矩阵运算的应用程序来说是一个重要的进步，特别是在图算法、机器学习、仿真以及计算生物学等领域。

Abstract: The multiplication of two sparse matrices, known as SpGEMM, is a key kernel in scientific computing and large-scale data analytics, underpinning graph algorithms, machine learning, simulations, and computational biology, where sparsity is often highly unstructured. The unstructured sparsity makes achieving high performance challenging because it limits both memory efficiency and scalability. In distributed memory, the cost of exchanging and merging partial products across nodes further constrains performance. These issues are exacerbated on modern heterogeneous supercomputers with deep, hierarchical GPU interconnects. Current SpGEMM implementations overlook the gap between intra-node and inter-node bandwidth, resulting in unnecessary data movement and synchronization not fully exploiting the fast intra-node interconnect. To address these challenges, we introduce Trident, a hierarchy-aware 2D distributed SpGEMM algorithm that uses communication-avoiding techniques and asynchronous communication to exploit the hierarchical and heterogeneous architecture of modern supercomputing interconnect. Central to Trident is the novel trident partitioning scheme, which enables hierarchy-aware decomposition and reduces internode communication by leveraging the higher bandwidth between GPUs within a node compared to across nodes. Here, we evaluate Trident on unstructured matrices, achieving up to $2.38\times$ speedup over a 2D SpGEMM with a corresponding geometric mean speedup of $1.54\times$. Trident reduces internode communication volume by up to $2\times$ on NERSC's Perlmutter supercomputer. Furthermore, we demonstrate the effectiveness of Trident in speeding up Markov Clustering, achieving up to $2\times$ speedup compared to competing strategies.

</details>


### [94] [exaCB: Reproducible Continuous Benchmark Collections at Scale Leveraging an Incremental Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22251)
*Jayesh Badwaik,Mathis Bode,Michal Rajski,Andreas Herten*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出了exaCB框架，用于高性能计算系统中的持续基准测试，支持大规模系统级研究和应用团队将基准测试集成到其工作流程中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着高性能计算（HPC）系统的异构性增加以及向exascale架构的转变，需要对不同工作负载进行系统且可重复的性能评估。虽然持续集成（CI）保证了软件工程中的功能正确性，但HPC中的性能和能效通常在CI工作流之外进行评估，这促使采用持续基准测试（CB）作为补充方法。

Method: 开发了一个名为exaCB的框架，它允许应用程序团队将基准测试集成到他们的工作流程中，并通过可重用的CI/CD组件、已建立的测试套件和共享报告协议支持大规模、系统范围的研究。该框架支持逐步采用，使得基准可以轻松加入并从基本的可运行性发展为更高级的工具化和再现性。

Result: 在JUPITER的早期访问计划JUREAP中展示了这种方法，其中exaCB使超过70个处于不同成熟度级别的应用程序能够进行连续基准测试，支持跨应用程序分析、性能跟踪和能源意识研究。

Conclusion: 这些结果表明，对于跨越大型、多样化科学应用集合的exascale HPC系统而言，使用exaCB进行持续基准测试是可行的。

Abstract: The increasing heterogeneity of high-performance computing (HPC) systems and the transition to exascale architectures require systematic and reproducible performance evaluation across diverse workloads. While continuous integration (CI) ensures functional correctness in software engineering, performance and energy efficiency in HPC are typically evaluated outside CI workflows, motivating continuous benchmarking (CB) as a complementary approach. Integrating benchmarking into CI workflows enables reproducible evaluation, early detection of regressions, and continuous validation throughout the software development lifecycle.
  We present exaCB, a framework for continuous benchmarking developed in the context of the JUPITER exascale system. exaCB enables application teams to integrate benchmarking into their workflows while supporting large-scale, system-wide studies through reusable CI/CD components, established harnesses, and a shared reporting protocol. The framework supports incremental adoption, allowing benchmarks to be onboarded easily and to evolve from basic runnability to more advanced instrumentation and reproducibility. The approach is demonstrated in JUREAP, the early-access program for JUPITER, where exaCB enabled continuous benchmarking of over 70 applications at varying maturity levels, supporting cross-application analysis, performance tracking, and energy-aware studies. These results illustrate the practicality using exaCB for continuous benchmarking for exascale HPC systems across large, diverse collections of scientific applications.

### [95] [FIGURA: A Modular Prompt Engineering Method for Artistic Figure Photography in Safety-Filtered Text-to-Image Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20201)
*Luca Cazzaniga*

Main category: cs.MM

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 系统测试揭示了几个先前未记录的发现：(1) 安全过滤器主要检测缺失描述而非存在描述；(2) 艺术家参考同时作为美学指南和改变过滤器行为的安全锚点；(3) 空间上下文作为一个独立的过滤变量工作；(4) 在轮廓上下文中几何词汇用于身体描述可以绕过模式识别。五个结构化的提示模板之间实现了80%到90%的成功率。

Abstract: Safety filters in commercial text-to-image (T2I) models systematically block legitimate artistic content involving the human figure, treating classical nude photography with the same restrictiveness as explicit material. While prior research has documented this problem extensively, no operational system exists that enables professional artists to generate artistic figure photography within the constraints of active safety filters. We present the FIGURA Method (Framework for Intelligent Generation of Unrestricted Artistic Results), a modular prompt engineering system comprising eight interconnected knowledge files, empirically validated through 200+ documented generation tests on FLUX 2 Pro (Cloud) with active safety filters at the default tolerance level. Our systematic testing reveals several previously undocumented findings: (1) safety filters primarily detect absence descriptions (references to missing clothing) rather than presence descriptions (references to body form), which we formalize as the Golden Rule; (2) artistic references to painters function simultaneously as aesthetic guides and as safety anchors that alter filter behavior; (3) spatial context operates as an independent filter variable, with documented success rate hierarchies; and (4) geometric vocabulary for body description bypasses pattern recognition in silhouette contexts. The system achieves documented success rates between 80% and 90% across five structured prompt templates, demonstrating that the artistic censorship problem identified in recent literature admits practical, systematic solutions that work with active safety mechanisms rather than circumventing them.

### [96] [Leum-VL Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20354)
*Yuxuan He,Chaiming Huang,Yifan Wu,Hongjun Wang,Chenkui Shen,Jifan Zhang,Long Li*

Main category: cs.MM

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为SV6D的结构化视频表示框架，旨在解决当前多模态模型在解析和生成短视频时缺乏结构性语法的问题。基于此框架，研究人员开发了Leum-VL-8B，一个实现了SV6D目标的80亿参数视频-语言模型，并通过专业驱动的后训练流程及可验证强化学习进一步优化。实验结果表明，在多个基准测试中Leum-VL-8B表现优异，强调了时间线基础上的结构性表征对于视频AI的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态模型能够描述场景、回答以事件为中心的问题以及读取屏幕上的文本，但在识别基于时间轴的关键单元（如吸引点、剪辑理由、镜头引起的紧张感及面向平台的包装提示）方面不够可靠。因此，需要一种新的方法来理解和生成视频内容中的这些结构性元素。

Method: 提出了受电影电视制作中专业故事板实践启发的SV6D框架，将互联网原生视频分解为主体、美学、摄像语言、编辑、叙事和传播六个互补的结构维度；每个标签都与时间轴上可观察到的物理证据相关联。接着，定义了一个统一的优化目标函数，结合匈牙利匹配的时间对齐、维度级语义标签距离以及质量正则化。基于此框架构建了Leum-VL-8B模型，并通过专家指导下的后训练流水线和感知导向任务上的可验证强化学习进行细化。

Result: Leum-VL-8B模型在VideoMME（无字幕）、MVBench和MotionBench等基准测试中分别取得了70.8分、70.0分和61.6分的成绩，同时在MMBench-EN等通用多模态评估中保持竞争力。此外，还构建了FeedBench作为结构敏感型短视频理解的新基准。

Conclusion: 研究表明，视频AI中缺失的一环并非像素生成而是结构性表征：即基于时间轴、与可见证据相联系且可以直接被下游工作流所使用的表征形式。这种结构性表征对于编辑、检索、推荐和生成控制等领域至关重要，特别是对于包含大量文本叠加和图文布局的互联网视频格式而言。

Abstract: A short video succeeds not simply because of what it shows, but because of how it schedules attention -- yet current multimodal models lack the structural grammar to parse or produce this organization. Existing models can describe scenes, answer event-centric questions, and read on-screen text, but they are far less reliable at identifying timeline-grounded units such as hooks, cut rationales, shot-induced tension, and platform-facing packaging cues.
  We propose SV6D (Structured Video in Six Dimensions), inspired by professional storyboard practice in film and television production, a representation framework that decomposes internet-native video into six complementary structural dimensions -- subject, aesthetics, camera language, editing, narrative, and dissemination -- with each label tied to physically observable evidence on the timeline. We formalize a unified optimization objective over SV6D that combines Hungarian-matched temporal alignment, dimension-wise semantic label distance, and quality regularization. Building on this framework, we present Leum-VL-8B, an 8B video-language model that realizes the SV6D objective through an expert-driven post-training pipeline, further refined through verifiable reinforcement learning on perception-oriented tasks.
  Leum-VL-8B achieves 70.8 on VideoMME (w/o subtitles), 70.0 on MVBench, and 61.6 on MotionBench, while remaining competitive on general multimodal evaluations such as MMBench-EN. We also construct FeedBench, a benchmark for structure-sensitive short-video understanding. Our results indicate that the missing layer in video AI is not pixel generation but structural representation: grounded on the timeline, linked to visible evidence, and directly consumable by downstream workflows such as editing, retrieval, recommendation, and generation control, including text-heavy internet video formats with overlays and image-text layouts.

</details>


### [97] [AcoustEmo: Open-Vocabulary Emotion Reasoning via Utterance-Aware Acoustic Q-Former](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20894)
